kyngdome mat xiii p thinges haue added fill vp leffe p infernus gehenna differ moche significacion though none interpretacion ether englyshe worde hell gehenna signifieth place punyshement infernus taken maner place beneth erth grave sepulchre cave hell called hebrue valeye ofmath v hennon place ierusalem burnt chyldren fyer vnto ydole moloch vsurped taken place wycked vngodlye shalbe tormented soule bodye generall iudgement geue rowme wrath god rom xiirom xxii wrath taken vengeaunce meaninge let god advenge ether himselfe officer beare rowme tarye abyde tyll ye go oute yt ismat x marke vi wheresoever ye enter house abyde till ye go oute thece luke ix soever housse ye enter ther tarye go oute thence saye whosoever receaveth abyde longe citie toune go shamefully beggynge housse housse freers dust shake dust youre fete matthewmat x x comaunded shake dust wytnes sayth luke dede maye testifie agaynst daye iudgement doctrine salvacion offered wolde receave ye se also soche gesture ceremony haue greater power bare wordes onlye move harte stere vp fayth layenge handes anoyntinge oyle c ypocrytes ye decerne face heaven decerne signe tymes saye coulde iudge signesmath xvi skye
